	USA_homeland_defense = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			original_tag = USA
		}

		available = {
			any_owned_state = {
				is_core_of = USA
				is_on_continent = north_america
				any_neighbor_state = {
					CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			surrender_progress > 0.01
			has_civil_war = no
			has_war_with_major = yes
		}

		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				is_core_of = USA
				is_on_continent = north_america
				any_neighbor_state = {
					CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			CSA = {
				exists = no
			}
		}

		cost = 0
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10000
		}

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_support < 0.9
				}
				set_war_support = 0.9
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = USA_great_depression
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = USA_great_depression
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = extensive_conscription
						has_idea = scraping_the_barrel
						has_idea = service_by_requirement
						has_idea = all_adults_serve
					}
				}
				add_ideas = extensive_conscription
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = undisturbed_isolation
						has_idea = isolation
						has_idea = civilian_economy
						has_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
					}
				}
				add_ideas = war_economy
			}
			add_ideas = USA_homeland_defense
		}
	}

			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_soviet_aid_otw }
		}

        fire_only_once = yes

        modifier = {
            civilian_factory_use = 40
        }

		cost = 5
		days_remove = 120

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 400
		}

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = USA_soviet_aid_otw
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = USA_soviet_aid_otw
			economy_fatigue_level_up_4 = yes
            if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = { controls_state = 571 }
				}

					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 35
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
            }
		}
	}

			NOT = { has_war_with = JAP }
			JAP = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = embargoed_by_USA }
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 50

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 4000

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				JAP = { has_government = democratic }
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_embargo_japan_tt2
			hidden_effect = {
				JAP = {
					set_country_flag = embargoed_by_USA
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_opinion_modifier = improved_relations_ai
					}
					remove_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = improved_relations_ai }
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = JAP
							is_in_faction_with = JAP
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
					}
					add_to_temp_array = {
						temp_JAP_faction = THIS
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							AND = {
								is_guaranteed_by = USA

		}

			base = 0

			modifier = {
				add = 400
				OR = {

									tag = JAP

								}

						}

			}
		}

				}
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						is_on_continent = north_america
						is_on_continent = south_america
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_civil_war = yes
					AND = {
						is_subject = yes
						NOT = { tag = DEG }
						NOT = { tag = CAN }
						NOT = { tag = UKW }
						NOT = { tag = UKO }
						NOT = { tag = DWI }
						NOT = { tag = FRI }
						NOT = { tag = FRO }
						OVERLORD = {
							NOT = {
								capital_scope = {
									OR = {
										is_on_continent = north_america
										is_on_continent = south_america
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 50
		days_remove = 35
		war_with_target_on_remove = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			create_wargoal = {
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
				target = FROM
			}
		}
	}
	USA_demand_liberation = {
		available = {
			has_war_support > 0.2
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_support > 0.6
				}
				congress_low_support_trigger = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_support > 0.4
				}
				congress_medium_support_trigger = yes
			}
			else = {
				congress_high_support_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = USA_reinforce_monroe_doctrine
			NOT = { has_wargoal_against = FROM }
			FROM = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_monroe_backed_down } #set when US player backs down in reply event
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = PREV
					OR = {
						is_on_continent = north_america
						is_on_continent = south_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					original_tag = FRA
				}
				NOT = {
					original_tag = VIC
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_government = ROOT
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					capital_scope = {
						OR = {
							is_on_continent = north_america
							is_on_continent = south_america
						}
					}
				}
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = PREV
					OR = {
						is_on_continent = north_america
						is_on_continent = south_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 50
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = mtg_usa_diplomatic_protest.2
			}
		}
	}

					}

						random_core_state = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									region = 119
									region = 120
									region = 119
									region = 199
									region = 209
								}
								is_core_of = USA
								is_on_continent = north_america

									size > 0
								}

										controller = {
											NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
										}
										is_controlled_by = USA
									}
								}
							}
							add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
							add_building_construction = {
								type = synthetic_refinery
								level = 1
								instant_build = yes

	USA_stop_the_industry_relocation = {

		allowed = {
            original_tag = USA
        }

        cost = 0
        fire_only_once = no

        available = {
			NOT = {
				surrender_progress > 0
				any_owned_state = {
					is_core_of = USA
					is_on_continent = north_america
					any_neighbor_state = {
						CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
        }

        visible = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_stop_industry_relocation
			}
			has_completed_focus = USA_victory_at_all_costs
        }

        complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_stop_industry_relocation
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	USA_resume_the_industry_relocation = {

		allowed = {
            original_tag = USA
        }

        cost = 0
        fire_only_once = no

        available = {
			any_owned_state = {
				is_core_of = USA
				is_on_continent = north_america
				any_neighbor_state = {
					CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			surrender_progress > 0
        }

        visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_stop_industry_relocation
			has_completed_focus = USA_victory_at_all_costs
        }

        complete_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = USA_stop_industry_relocation
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}


USA_scorched_earth_category = {
	USA_scorched_earth = {

		icon = generic_scorched_earth

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = {
				is_core_of = USA
				is_on_continent = north_america
				is_controlled_by = USA
				OR = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					}
					NOT = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_state_flag = USA_scorched_earth_flag }
			}
		}

		available = {
			has_war = yes
			any_owned_state = {
				is_core_of = USA
				is_on_continent = north_america
				is_controlled_by = USA
				OR = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					}
					NOT = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_state_flag = USA_scorched_earth_flag }
			}
		}

		cost = 0

		fire_only_once = no

		visible = {
			surrender_progress > 0
			has_completed_focus = USA_victory_at_all_costs
		}

		days_remove = 10

		remove_effect = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = USA
					is_on_continent = north_america
					is_controlled_by = USA
					OR = {
						any_neighbor_state = {
							CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT }
						}
						NOT = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_state_flag = USA_scorched_earth_flag }
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = rail_way
					damage = 5
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 5
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = supply_node
					damage = 1
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = air_base
					damage = 10
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = naval_base
					damage = 5
				}
				set_state_flag = USA_scorched_earth_flag
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 500
		}
	}
}
